of the financial statements and for being\nsatisfied that they give a true and fair view.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our responsibility is to audit and express an\nopinion on the financial statements in accordance with\napplicable law and International Standards on Auditing (UK\nand Ireland).<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Those standards require us\nto comply with the Auditing Practices Board's Ethical\nStandards for Auditors.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Scope of the audit of the\nfinancial statements</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">An audit involves\nobtaining evidence about the amounts and disclosures in the financial statements sufficient to give reasonable assurance that the\nfinancial statements are free from material misstatement,\nwhether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This\nincludes an assessment of: whether the accounting policies\nare appropriate to the company's circumstances and have been\nconsistently applied and adequately disclosed; the reasonableness of\nsignificant accounting estimates made by the directors; and\nthe overall presentation of the financial statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>In addition, we read all the financial and\nnon-financial information in the Annual Report to identify\nmaterial inconsistencies with the audited financial statements and to identify\nany information that is materially incorrect based on, or materially inconsistent with, the knowledge acquired by us in the course\nof performing the audit. If we become aware of any apparent\nmaterial misstatements or inconsistencies we consider the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest receivable and payable are\nrecognised on an accruals basis in the period in which they fall due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investment\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment properties are revalued\nannually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for Investment Properties)\nno provision is made for depreciation. This departure from the requirements of\nthe statutory accounting rules, which requires all properties to be depreciated\nis, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for the accounts to show a true\nand fair view. Depreciation is only one of the factors reflected in the annual\nvaluation and the amount attributable to this factor is not capable of being\nseparately identified or quantified. Surpluses or deficits are transferred to\nthe revaluation reserve, unless a deficit exceeds previous surpluses recognised\non the same property, in which case the excess is charged to the profit and\nloss account.</span></p></div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;&#xD;&#xA;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:&#xD;&#xA;AR-SA\"><br /></span><div class=\"WordSection10\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other\ndebtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors are recognised initially at fair\nvalue.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A provision for impairment is\nestablished where there is objective evidence that the company will not be able\nto collect all amounts due according to the original terms of the debtor\nconcerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other\ncreditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade and other\ncreditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Debt</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt instruments are stated initially at\nthe amount of the net proceeds. The finance costs of such debt instruments are\nallocated to periods over the term of the debt at a constant rate on the\ncarrying amount. The carrying amount is increased by the finance cost in\nrespect of the reporting period and reduced by payments made in respect of the\ndebt of that period. Finance costs are charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current tax is provided at amounts\nexpected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates and laws that have been\nenacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet date. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax assets and liabilities\narise from timing differences between the recognition of gains and losses in\nthe financial statements and their recognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under FRS 19 deferred tax is recognised\nin respect of all timing differences that have originated but not reversed at\nthe balance sheet date where transactions or events that result in an\nobligation to pay more tax in the future or a right to pay less tax in the\nfuture have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as recoverable and therefore recognised\nonly when, on the basis of all available evidence, it can be regarded as more\nlikely than not that there will be suitable taxable profits from which the\nfuture reversal of the underlying timing differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is not recognised when\nfixed assets are revalued unless by the balance sheet date there is a binding\nagreement to sell the revalued assets and the gain or loss expected to arise on\nsale has been recognised in the financial statements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is measured on a discounted\nbasis to reflect the time value of money over the period between the balance\nsheet date and the dates on which it is estimated that the timing differences\nwill reverse, or where the timing differences are not expected to reverse, a\nperiod not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount\nrates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been adopted reflecting the post-tax yield to\nmaturity that can be obtained on government bonds with similar maturity dates\nand currencies to those of the deferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule:&#xD;&#xA;exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p></div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;&#xD;&#xA;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:&#xD;&#xA;AR-SA\"><br /></span><div class=\"WordSection11\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span the company\nduring the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>No staff were\nemployed by the company during the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span has been borne by another\ngroup undertaking.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">3.</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>INTEREST\nRECEIVABLE AND SIMILAR INCOME</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes\"><td valign=\"top\" style=\"width:268.55pt;padding:0in 1.25pt 0in 1.25pt\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\"
